2154 French Physicians, Military Men and Executives. Serie E, volume 1 : from 1901 to 1963
 

BIRTH AND PLANETARY DATA GATHERED SINCE 1949
(Coordonnées natales et planétaires rassemblées depuis 1949)

Series E: New Birth Data Series (Volume 1)
by Michel et Françoise GAUQUELIN

© Laboratoire d'Étude des Relations entre Rythmes Cosmiques et Psychophysiologiques
L.E.R.R.C.P., Paris, 1984 ; C.U.R.A. (http://cura.free.fr), 2001 ; 2009

[2nd CURA's edition, revised by Patrice Guinard : February 2009]
 

Notice

NUM : Number (from 1 to 2145 ; 11 items have been added but n. 285 & n. 1155 are omitted)
PRO : Profession
NAME : Name
DAY : Day of birth
MON : Month of birth
YEA : Year of birth
H : Hour of birth (Birth certificate)
CITY : Place of birth
COD : Abbreviated Code of Birth place indicating the French "Département"
 

Date ant time of birth were obtained from the registry office of the place of birth indicated in the WHO'S WHO IN FRANCE (1955-56 and 1975-76 editions).
 

Codes of Professions

975 PHysicians (PH)
629 Military Man (MI)
549 top EXecutives (EX)
 

Physicians : A plus sign (+) is added before the names of the physicians elected members of the French Academies of Medicine or Sciences. A minus sign (-) is printed before the names of doctors of apparent lesser stature than the other listed.

Military men : The letter L is added before the name of people also awarded "compagnon de la libération".

An asterisk (*) is added before the names of the very few people (64 out of 2145, i.e. 3 percent) who were taken from other sources than the WHO'S WHO (essentially cases forgotten in our previous study and restored here, and forty military leaders from the library of the Musée de l'Armée in Paris).

The position of the Moon (MO), Venus (VE), Mars (MA), Jupiter (JU) and Saturn (SA) in the 36 "Gauquelin Sectors" are given in an addenda.
